66.1(1): 'dzin med bon nyid dbyings su dag /rang 'byung ye shes phur pa bya/ rdzu 'phrul

66.11(1): le'u ste so gcig pa'o// //

84.18(1): dbyings las/ skye ba med la rdzu 'phrul sku/ 'gag med nam mkhar nyi ma shar/ phyi 
84.19(1): nang med par 'od po che/ mtshan ma'i rnam rtog zil gyis gnon/ gsum dang lnga 
84.20(1): dang grangs med pa/ che ba'i yon tan mdzes pa'i rgyan/ sku gsum lhun grub dpe 
84.21(1): byad bzang / mtshan dpe yon tan zad med mdzod/ mkhyen pa'i ye shes rtogs pa'i 
85.1(1): phul/ thabs kyi rgyal po 'gro 'dul sku/ log rtog mtshan ma 'joms pa'i dpung / skye 
85.2(1): med dbyings la longs spyod rgyan/ sprul sku grangs med bsam las 'das/ bsam 
85.3(1): gyis mi khyab brjod mi long / zhi rgyas dbang drag mngon spyod du/ rigs dang sde tshan 
85.4(1): zhing khams bcas/ so sor sprul zhing gnyen por shar/ smra bsam brjod dang bral 
85.5(1): ba la/ thugs kyi klong brdol pad+ma'i lces/ brgyad khri bzhi stong bon gyi sgo/ brgyud lung 
85.6(1): man ngag bsam las 'das/ drang don nges don ston pa'i bka'/ rang gsal theg 
85.7(1): pa rgyu'i bon/ bka' yi bye brag phun sum tshogs/ gang ltar dad mos gnyen po shar/
85.8(1): rang 'byung ye shes thams cad mkhyen/ rnam rtog mi mnga' dran rig thugs/ rgyu rkyen 
85.9(1): med pa'i snying po nyid/ ma bcos kun gzhi byang chub sems/ stong zhing bdag med 
85.10(1): bon gyi dbyings/ phyi nang kun gsal rtog pa med/ phyogs ris med pa mnyam pa'i 
85.11(1): ngang / spyi dang rang rig mtshan nyid 'dzin/ bya brtsal med pa grub pa'i las/ rang 
85.12(1): bzhin 'od gsal rnam par dag /ye shes 'od zer gsal ba'i mdangs/ ma sgrib 
85.13(1): ye shes mkhyen pa'i mdzod/ dbang dang byin rlabs dngos grub gter/ mi rtogs 
85.14(1): 'gro 'dul thabs la mkhas/ ma rig dug 'joms gnyen por shar/ rang 'byung 
85.15(1): yon tan phun sum tshogs/ yid bzhin nor bu 'phrul po che/ ye shes 'od zer che 
85.16(1): ba'i rgyan/ gser gyi nyi ma rang 'byung sku/ 'khor lo bsgyur ba'i stobs po che/ lhun 
85.17(1): grub yon tan rang dag gsal/ legs pa kun 'byung thugs rjer grub/ nam mkha'i 
85.18(1): dbyings dang rgya mtsho'i klong / nub pa med pa'i snying por gsal/ che'o yangs so 
85.19(1): yon tan mchog /kun snyoms yon tan snying po shar/ khyab bdal lhun grub ye shes 
85.20(1): che/ mdzad pa rnam dag phun sum tshogs/ bya bral rtsol sgrub bral ba'i rdeng / 'phrin 
85.21(1): las mthar phyin lhun gyis grub/ mdzad spyod thabs kyi ye shes kyi/ zhen chags med 
86.1(1): pa'i dbyings su sbyor/ kun grub 'phrin las gnyen po shar/ nyon mongs rang grol 
86.2(1): dug lnga rtsad gcod kyi rgyud las/ gnyen po ye shes kyi gnas lugs bstan pa'i le'u 
86.3(1): ste gsum pa'o// //
86.4(1): 7 dus gsum 'gyur med g.yung drung sems/ bskal par mi nub rgyal mtshan 
86.5(1): can/ srid par 'khyams kyang sems mi stor/ 'byung ba 'khrug kyang yid mi bsgribs/
86.6(1): dus gsum bral kyang dbyings mi nyams/ stong gsum 'gyur kyang klong mi 'gag /
86.7(1): khams gsum 'thib kyang mkha' mi bsgribs/ rang gsal rang stong 'gyur ba med/
86.8(1): skad cig gcig la rdzogs mnyam nyid/ rang gsal rang 'byung ye shes nyid/ stong 
86.9(1): pa bon nyid dbyings su grol/ de gsum mi phyed gcig gi ngang / mnyam nyid phyogs 
86.10(1): ris med par gnas/ brtsal du med pa'i ye shes che/ 'du 'bral med pa lhun 
86.11(1): grub gnas/ rtag chad mtha' bral chen por dag /dag pa nyid kyang dag la 'das/
86.12(1): 'das pa'i bon la bshad du med/ dper na nam mkha'i ngog dbyings ltar/ mi 
86.13(1): mthun gang dang mthun pa la/ yin ni cir yang ma yin par/ 'char ni cir yang 
86.14(1): 'char ba la/ grub ni mtshan mar ma grub pa/ mtha' mar ltung ba'i ye shes nyid/
86.15(1): 'phel 'grib med pa'i ngo bor gnas/ lta ba'i don gnas rang sa zin/ nyon mongs 
86.16(1): rang grol chen po yis/ dug lnga rang gi rtsa ba chod/ rnam rtog chu bran rka chad 'dra/
86.17(1): 'khor ba'i zhing sa dbyings su thim/ srid pa mi nub g.yung drung sems/ phyogs su 
86.18(1): ma ltung lta ba'i gnas/ gzhi rtsa med pa'i snying po la/ gzugs su ma grub mtshan ma 
86.19(1): med/ phung po byang sems mngon par shes/ smra bsam brjod dang bral ba la/ dran 
86.20(1): rig mi 'khrul g.yung drung thugs/ che ba'i yon tan sprul pa'i rgyan/ rtsol sgrub med 
86.21(1): par spyod las 'das/ rang 'byung rig pa spyi blugs shar/ bon sku'i rtsa ba byang chub 
87.1(1): sems/ sems la ma gtogs bon rnams med/ sems nyid rtogs pa'i khyad par 
87.2(1): la/ che ba'i yon tan rtsal ma 'gag /mya ngan 'das pa'i bon du shar/ sems nyid

87.6(1): stong du ga la 'dod/ rnam par rtog pa 'gag pa med/ mya ngan 'da' ba gang zhig 
87.7(1): 'ong / gzhig pa'i dngos po grol mi 'gyur/ sems nyid gsas mkhar med pa min/
87.8(1): med na rig pa ci ltar 'char/ rnam pa thams cad ci ltar mkhyen/ 'khor ba rgyu drug 
87.9(1): ltung mi srid/ thar pa'i 'bras bu lam mi rnyed/ sems nyid gsas mkhar gnyis ka 
87.10(1): min/ yin na gnyis su 'drer ('dres )mi rung / rnam rtog mi mnga' cir yang gsal/
87.11(1): gsal la mi rtog 'byung mi 'gyur/ sems nyid gsas mkhar gnyis med min/ yin 
87.12(1): na rtogs dang ma rtogs dang / 'khor ba mya ngan 'das pa dang / gnyen po nyon 
87.13(1): mongs 'byung mi 'gyur/ rang bzhin lhun grub snying po nyid/ mkha' klong dbyings 
87.14(1): kyi gsas mkhar du/ ci yang ma yin cir yang 'char/ ma grub ma 'gag gcig la 
87.15(1): rdzogs/ zhen pa'i sgros 'dog skur 'debs med/ kun grol gsas mkhar chen po 
87.16(1): ste/ nub pa med pa'i rgyal mtshan can/ dper na nam mkha' khyung chen bzhin/ spyi 
87.17(1): rgya rlabs kyis chod par gnas/ / mkha' la nyi ma shar ba ltar/ kun la gsal zhing 
87.18(1): snyoms par gnas/ rgya mtsho chen po'i klong yangs ltar/ phyi nang snod bcud rdzogs 
87.19(1): par gnas/ nyon mongs rang grol dug lnga rtsad gcod kyi rgyud las/ lta ba rang grol 
87.20(1): bstan pa'i le'u ste bzhi pa'o// //
87.21(1): 7 g.yung drung ye khebs gsas mkhar lta ba la/ gar yang mi btsal spyod pa kun 
88.1(1): las 'das/ dmigs med mi g.yo rang sems ye thub tu/ dbyings nas mi nyams

88.10(1): su bzhag /mi g.yo dbyings la kun 'byung klong 'khrug ste/ mkha' la log par snang

88.12(1): bdag bcing gzung bas gzhan bcing nas/ gsas mkhar g.yung drung sems kyi 
88.13(1): don mi gsal/ rtsol bas bya brtsal 'khrul pa'i dmag gseb tu/ dmyal ba'i grong 
88.14(1): bzung ngan song btson du khrid/ thar pa'i lam bral byang chub sems dang 'gyangs /

88.16(1): nas sprugs pa'i phyir/ g.yung drung ye khyab gsas mkhar snying po ru/ gar spyin rtsi la 
88.17(1): snang (sbrang)ma chags pa bzhin/ dbyings dang rig pa gnyis med ngang la gnas/ ma 
88.18(1): yengs mi 'gyur don gsal lhun grub gnas/ 'bras bu brtsal med rnam pa thams

88.21(1): 7 lta dgongs gnyis med 'du 'bral med pa ru/ snang ba rang grol rang shar

93.21(1): rang gol da bstan pa'i le' sre brgad pa'o// //
94.1(1): 7 ma byung ma g.yos thugs mchog las/ srid pa'i snying po 'bras bu mchog /

140.19(1): dbyings kyi lha lnga longs spyod rdzogs/ lnga las 'phrin las mthar phyin pa/ gzi brjid

140.21(1): sku stod zhal gsum phyag drug pa/ me ri 'bar ba'i gshog pa can/ sked pa ye shes rgya

141.8(1): gting nas len/ sku ni bdud bzhi 'joms pa'i sku/ mi mthun log lta zil gyis

141.18(1): bstan pa'i le'u ste so brgyad pa'o/ //
141.19(1): 7 stong zhing bdag med bon gyi dbyings/ ye nas ma bcos de bzhin nyid/ rang 
141.20(1): dag mtshan ma med pa la/ tshad med thugs rje rgyun 'byung pa/ ma rtogs sems can 
141.21(1): kun la khyab/ thugs rje gsal rdzogs ngo bo ru/ rang snang rig pa'i ye shes la/ e yaM 
142.1(1): raM baM su raM hU~M/ bskyed bskul sngags kyi nam mkha' la/ rim brtsegs ri rab gzhal 
142.2(1): yas khang / swa tri ya na k+sha dag las/ rang rang khri gdan rdzogs pa'o/ /e raM kha raM 
142.3(1): ta raM tsha raM pha raM 'od zer las/ sku bskyed sngags kyi 'phro 'du yi/ gzi byin drag po 
142.4(1): khro bo'i tshogs/ yab yum khra thabs sprul pa dang / pho nya las mkhan srung ma'i bskor/

142.6(1): gting rdzogs phur pa'i lha/ dpa' bo kun sgrol phyag rgya bsgom/ rang snang dam tshig 
142.7(1): gsal rdzogs pa/ bdag gi sras su sprul zhing bskyed/ bdag nyid lha'i ngo bo yi/

142.9(1): sems dpa'i dkyil 'khor lha/ ting 'dzin 'od zer lcags kyu'i mtshon/ mchod pa'i 
142.10(1): lha mo spyan drangs shing / rang snang dam tshig dkyil 'khor la/ bye ma la ni mar thim 
142.11(1): ltar/ dbyer med gcig gi ngang du bstim/ gnyis su med par gtan dam bcas/

142.13(1): snying po rgyun du drangs/ dgongs pa gsal ba'i 'phro 'du bya/ rtags la phebs nas

143.4(1): 7 ma rtogs 'khrul pa'i sems can la/ 'khor ba'i lte ba ma rig pa/ nyon mongs

504.1(1): mthar don du nged [<<]g.yung drung bon gyi bka' brten dpe rnying phyogs bsgrigs khang [>>]
504.2(1): gis las don rlabs chen 'di 'dra zhig legs grub byung ba ni/ rig gzhung 'di dang 
504.3(1): bstan pa 'di la lhag bsam can gyis phyar gru mnyam 'degs byas pa las byung ba 
504.4(1): yin/ kan su'u mi rigs dpe skrun khang gi dbu khrid 'brug rgyal mkhar dang gcod pa 
504.5(1): rnam gnyis nas thugs khur rgyab skyor tshad med gnang ba dang / lhag par du dus rab 
504.6(1): kyi gnyan 'phrang mang po'i nang tshe srog 'ben dang bsdos te srung skyong byas pa'i dpe cha 
504.7(1): g.yar ba'i dpe bdag rnam pa dang / de bzhin nga tsho'i bstan don gyi bya ba kun la 
504.8(1): mthun sbyor gnang ba ma tshad dpe tshogs 'di dpar skrun skabs su yang ma bskul dang 
504.9(1): blang gis zhal 'debs gnang mkhan bcas dngos shugs brgyud gsum nas rgyu tshegs 
504.10(1): thabs gsum gyis sdong grogs rogs ram gnang mkhan yongs la snying dbus nas 
504.11(1): thugs rje che zhu rgyu dang / gsung rab dag bzhengs byas pa'i dge ba'i tshogs 'dis/
504.12(1): 7 skyabs rje rgyal ba sman ri ba'i mkhan slob rnam gnyis gtsos ris su ma chad pa'i 
504.13(1): bstan 'dzin skyes chen dam pa rnams kyi sku tshe bskal brgyar brtan zhing bzhed dgongs 
504.14(1): lhun gyis 'grub pa dang / 'brel thogs kyi sbyin pa'i bdag po dang las gzhi 'di'i byed 
504.15(1): po kun tshe bsod dbang khams gong nas gong du mtho ste myur du sku gsum rdzogs pa'i 
504.16(1): sangs rgyas kyi go 'phang thob pa dang / zhang bod rig gzhung rnams mi nyams gong nas 
504.17(1): gong du 'phel te 'dzam gling tha gru yongs kyi snod bcud rgud pa gso zhing phan bde'i 
504.18(1): gsos su khyab pa dang / yangs pa'i rgyal khams kun du nad mug 'khrug rtsod dang rang 
504.19(1): byung 'byung ba'i 'jigs pa rnams rmeng med du zhi nas bde legs phun tshogs skyid kyi nyi
